class="post-categories"><li><a href="https://thekatieshowblog.com/category/travel/" rel="category tag">Travel</a></li></ul></div><h1 class="cb-post-title"><a href="https://thekatieshowblog.com/best-place-to-stay-in-cappadocia-cave-hotel/" rel="bookmark">Best Place To Stay In Cappadocia &#8211; Here&#8217;s The Ultimate Cave Hotel</a></h1><div class="cb-post-meta"><ul><li>By <a href="https://thekatieshowblog.com/author/katiemcintosh1988hotmail-com/" title="Posts by Katie Mac" rel="author">Katie Mac</a></li><li>July 3, 2018</li><li>11 Comments</li></ul></div></div><div class="cb-post-content"><div style='display:none;' class='shareaholic-canvas' data-app='share_buttons' data-title='Best Place To Stay In Cappadocia - Here&#039;s The Ultimate Cave Hotel' data-link='https://thekatieshowblog.com/best-place-to-stay-in-cappadocia-cave-hotel/' data-app-id-name='post_above_content'></div><div class='mailmunch-forms-before-post' style='display: none !important;'></div><p style="text-align: justify;">UPDATED FEB 2020. Before we start, I want you to toss out any ideas of staying in a regular hotel room in Cappadocia. Staying in a cave hotel is the only option you need. I mean, why not? Where else can you sleep inside a cave that has been carved into a mountain?! When I was planning my trip I knew that I wanted to book a cave hotel. I spent a lot of time scrolling through all of the options &#8211; there are a lot to choose from. I ended up finding a great deal on <a href="https://www.booking.com/index.html?aid=1342563" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">Booking.Com</a> for this hotel so I jumped on it. Let&#8217;s take a closer look at the best place to stay in Cappadocia. Of course, if you have any questions, just let me know in the comments.</p><p><span id="more-6683"></span></p><h2 style="text-align: center;">Best Place To Stay In Cappadocia &#8211; Here&#8217;s The Ultimate Cave Hotel</h2><p><a href="https://thekatieshowblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Best-place-to-stay-in-Cappadocia-1.jpg"><img decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-16062" src="https://sp-ao.shortpixel.ai/client/to_webp,q_glossy,ret_img,w_500,h_750/https://thekatieshowblog.com/wp-content/plugins/a3-lazy-load/assets/images/lazy_placeholder.gif" data-lazy-type="image" data-src="https://sp-ao.shortpixel.ai/client/to_webp,q_glossy,ret_img,w_500,h_750/https://thekatieshowblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Best-place-to-stay-in-Cappadocia-1-200x300.jpg" alt="Toss out any ideas of staying in a regular hotel room because staying in a cave hotel is a must do. This means at no extra cost to you, I earn a commission if you book through the link.</em></p><h3 style="text-align: center;">Basic information for this cave hotel in Cappadocia</h3><p><strong>Location:</strong> Uçhisar</p><p><strong>How to book:</strong> <a href="https://www.booking.com/hotel/tr/rox-cappadocia.en.html?aid=1342563&amp;no_rooms=1&amp;group_adults=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">Book your stay at Rox Cappadocia here</a></p><p><strong>Good for:</strong> Solo travel, couples travel, friends</p><p><strong>Highlights:</strong> Epic rooftop with views of hot air balloons, breakfast, quiet location</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-6702" style="text-align: justify;">Let&#8217;s talk about the cave room for a second.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I stayed in the Premier Cave Suite and felt like a queen. The 350-year-old room was previously a cave stable which you can tell from the different shapes cut out into the walls. You&#8217;ll learn all about that on the tours you&#8217;ll do while visiting Cappadocia.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The room I had was a legit cave with no windows or anything.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">It made waking up in the morning a little hard because I wanted to cozy up in the dark and sleep in, but they do have other rooms upstairs which have a nice view of the hot air balloons that fly at sunrise.</p><p>As far as comfortability goes, I had a heavenly sleep each night in the cool, dark cave surrounded by a mountain of pillows.</p><p>The bathroom was exquisite with a huge tub as spacious as the bathroom itself and they even provide slippers to walk around in.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter balloons</h3><p style="text-align: justify;">Every great cave hotel in Cappadocia has to have an amazing rooftop view right?</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The nice thing about this hotel, in particular, is that it is higher up on the hill which allows for incredible views over the valley below.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Of course, this means there is also an incredible view of the famous morning flight of the hot air balloons.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I sat on the rooftop each morning and evening and it was the most relaxing way to start and end the day, much like the amazing rooftop at <a href="https://thekatieshowblog.com/where-to-stay-in-marrakech/">Riad Star in Marrakech</a>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I also had it all to myself each time which was a huge bonus but I might&#8217;ve just been lucky with that one.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-6704" src="https://www.instagram.com/embed.js"></script></p></div><h3>The breakfast</h3><p style="text-align: justify;">Turkish breakfasts are on another level.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">They are famous for generous spreads of fresh bread, olives, cakes, eggs, cheese, vegetables, and all sorts of other goodies.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Rox Cappadocia honors this famous hospitality well. Each morning breakfast is freshly prepared and it&#8217;s just so delicious!</p><p style="text-align: justify;">You will not go hungry either. There is a lot to try with a mix of foods you have probably eaten many times before as well as new foods you&#8217;ll be able to try.</p><div class='mailmunch-forms-in-post-middle' style='display: none !important;'></div><p style="text-align: justify;">Personally, I cringe at the &#8216;breakfast goals&#8217; types of photos you see all over Instagram because it&#8217;s clearly far too much food for one person and it&#8217;s so wasteful.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I let the staff know they could serve the same food to me each day if they wanted to avoid wasting it, and they advised that nothing is wasted. They give some to the local village and some to the animals in the area.</p><h3>Add a personal touch to your stay</h3><p style="text-align: justify;">If you want to add more meaning to your stay, get a copy of my latest book &#8220;<a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B08LJZLPRQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B08LJZLPRQ&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=thkashbl-20&amp;linkId=a28811876445a8d01aed3525bcd989f4" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Your Vacation, My Office</a><img class="lazy lazy-hidden" loading="lazy" decoding="async" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" src="https://sp-ao.shortpixel.ai/client/to_webp,q_glossy,ret_img,w_1,h_1/https://thekatieshowblog.com/wp-content/plugins/a3-lazy-load/assets/images/lazy_placeholder.gif" data-lazy-type="image" data-src="//ir-na.amazon-adsystem.com/e/ir?t=thkashbl-20&amp;l=am2&amp;o=1&amp;a=B08LJZLPRQ" alt="" width="1" height="1" border="0" /><noscript><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" style="border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;" src="//ir-na.amazon-adsystem.com/e/ir?t=thkashbl-20&amp;l=am2&amp;o=1&amp;a=B08LJZLPRQ" alt="" width="1" height="1" border="0" /></noscript>.&#8221;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">It profiles people who work in travel around the world and the owner of Rox Cappadocia, Arda, is featured. style="text-align: justify;">What&#8217;s great about the Rox is the small group of staff that welcome you.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The owner, Arda, was always around and each morning you could see him checking on everyone at breakfast to see if there was anything they needed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Not only do they perform the usual hotel tasks like serve breakfast and clean the room, but the staff can also arrange airport transport, book your tours, taxis, and activities and they were always happy to help with anything I needed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I cannot say enough good things about the team.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-6705" style="text-align: justify;">To be honest, I didn&#8217;t realize why the location of this hotel made it one of the best places to stay in Cappadocia.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">It wasn&#8217;t until after I had been on the day tours and talked to other travelers that I realized how good the location was.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Mainly, because it&#8217;s not in the main city of Göreme.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">A few of the other travelers I met mentioned that their hotels in Göreme were great, but the location wasn&#8217;t ideal because there was a lot of noise each night.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">If you want to be right in the city, <a href="https://www.booking.com/searchresults.en.html?city=-750642&amp;aid=1342563&amp;no_rooms=1&amp;group_adults=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">then choose Göreme</a>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">The Rox has a sister hotel you can <a href="https://www.booking.com/hotel/tr/rox-goreme.html?aid=1342563&amp;no_rooms=1&amp;group_adults=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">take a look at here</a>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">If you want a place where you can be close to everything but away from the noise, then the Rox is a great choice because it was so quiet and peaceful.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-6711" Cappadocia</h3><p style="text-align: justify;">There are restaurants, markets, and stores all within walking distance and Göreme is only a 10-minute taxi away.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">I did a lot of walking around and shopping at the stores in the area you can get clothing, souvenirs, pottery, rugs and just about anything.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Don&#8217;t be surprised if you are invited for an apple tea while you shop.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">As with the staff at the Rox, the kind and hospitable people will do their best to make you feel welcome.</p><p><img
